    1626: Champions League Betting
    1628: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    2295: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them.     2342: Accumulators
    2344: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

    2684: Champions League Betting
    2686: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    2729: Doubles & Trebles
    2731: Fancy two or three teams to win? You can bet on both or all three happening for the chance to get even bigger odds by creating a double or treble.
    2733: Accumulators
    2735: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

2751: SW stands for "score and win". Betting on an SW market means you're simply betting on the match result and that both teams will score in the game. Or, you could choose a player to score and a team to win as part of a wincast.

    2755: Football betting guidance
    2756: Keep it fun: bet responsibly - as soon as it stops being fun, think about taking a step back.
    2757: Don't chase losses: never try to stretch your limits. Betting should be fun, so let's keep it that way.
    2758: Take a break: sometimes, everyone needs a breather. Taking a break can help keep a sense of balance.

    3079: Champions League Betting
    3081: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    3130: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

    3511: Doubles & Trebles
    3513: Fancy two or three teams to win? You can bet on both or all three happening for the chance to get even bigger odds by creating a double or treble.
    3515: Accumulators
    3517: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

3533: SW stands for "score and win". Betting on an SW market means you're simply betting on the match result and that both teams will score in the game. Or, you could choose a player to score and a team to win as part of a wincast.

    3537: Football betting guidance
    3538: Keep it fun: bet responsibly - as soon as it stops being fun, think about taking a step back.
    3539: Don't chase losses: never try to stretch your limits. Betting should be fun, so let's keep it that way.
    3540: Take a break: sometimes, everyone needs a breather. Taking a break can help keep a sense of balance.
    3541: Get support, if you need it: don't forget that you can talk to us at any time. Charities like GambleAware can help too.
    3542: Know your limits: set a budget - this will help you stay in control of what you spend, and keep betting fun.
    3543: Stay up-to-date with team news: give yourself an edge on the competition by knowing teams' strengths and weaknesses, as well as who's fit and who's injured.
